                 <div class="content-area-cont left relative">
                  <div class="sec-marg-out relative">

                      <div class="content-main left relative">
                       <div class="left relative prim-feat" id="featured-image">
                        <img itemprop="image" src="http://pocketviral.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/05/you-will-definitely-cry-while-wa.jpg"/>
                       </div>
                       <!--featured-image-->
                       <div class="theiaPostSlider_slides" id="tps_slideContainer_925">
                        <div>
                         <p>
                          <iframe allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="349" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/Z7dLU6fk9QY?feature=oembed" width="620">
                          </iframe>
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          How many Friends do you have onfacebook? But inspite of this doyou often feel Lonely?
                         </p>
                         <p>
                          Look up from your phone and Stop watching this Video. Give People your love and not your like!
                         </p>
                         <blockquote>
                          <p>
                           <span style="color: #000080;">
                            Look Up  A spoken word film for an online generation.
                           </span>
                           <br/>
                           <span style="color: #000080;">
                            Look Up is a lesson taught to us through a love story, in a world where we continue to find ways to make it easier for us to connect with one another, but always results in us spending more time alone.
                           </span>
                          </p>
                         </blockquote>
                         <pre>
                          <span style="color: #999999;">
                           Via:
                           <a class="g-hovercard yt-uix-sessionlink yt-user-name " data-name="watch" data-sessionlink="ei=TfF2U9HOO9XwuATc-YKYCw&amp;feature=watch" data-ytid="UCfHJe1XCvPckXPcgKh2V-5A" dir="ltr" href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCfHJe1XCvPckXPcgKh2V-5A" style="font-weight: bold;">
                            <span style="color: #999999;">
                             Gary Turk
                            </span>
                           </a>
                          </span>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   jQuery(document).ready(function($) {

	// Back to Top Button
    	var duration = 500;
    	$('.back-to-top').click(function(event) {
          event.preventDefault();
          $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: 0}, duration);
          return false;
    	})

	// Main Menu Dropdown Toggle
	$(".menu-item-has-children a").click(function(e){
	  e.stopPropagation();
	  location.href = this.href;
  	});

	$(".menu-item-has-children").click(function(){
    	  $(this).addClass('toggled');
    	  if($('.menu-item-has-children').hasClass('toggled'))
    	  {
    	  $(this).children('ul').toggle();
	  $(".main-menu").getNiceScroll().resize();
	  }
	  $(this).toggleClass('tog-minus');
    	  return false;
  	});

	// Main Menu Scroll
	$(window).load(function(){
	  $(".main-menu").niceScroll({cursorcolor:"#888",cursorwidth: 7,cursorborder: 0,zindex:999999});
	  $(".head-latest-wrap").niceScroll({cursorcolor:"#ccc",cursorwidth: 7,cursorborder: 0});
	});


	// Infinite Scroll
	$('.infinite-content').infinitescroll({
	  navSelector: ".nav-links",
	  nextSelector: ".nav-links a:first",
	  itemSelector: ".infinite-post",
	  loading: {
		msgText: "Loading more posts...",
		finishedMsg: "Sorry, no more posts"
	  }
	});

});
  </script>
